\\t\\t}\\n248: \\n249: \\t\\tselect {\\n250: \\t\\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\\n251: \\t\\tcase <-s.stopc:\\n252: \\t\\t\\treturn\\n253: \\t\\t}\\n254: \\t}\\n255: }\\n256: \\n257: // syncVictimsLoop tries to write precomputed watcher responses to\\n258: // watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\\n259: func (s *watchableStore) syncVictimsLoop() {\\n260: \\tdefer s.wg.Done()\\n261: \\n262: \\tfor {\\n263: \\t\\tfor s.moveVictims() != 0 {\\n264: \\t\\t\\t// try to update all victim watchers\\n265: \\t\\t}\\n266: \\t\\ts.mu.RLock()\\n267: \\t\\tisEmpty := len(s.victims) == 0\\n268: \\t\\ts.mu.RUnlock()\\n269: \\n270: \\t\\tvar tickc <-chan time.Time\\n271: \\t\\tif !isEmpty {\\n272: \\t\\t\\ttickc = time.After(10 * time.Millisecond)\\n273: \\t\\t}\\n274: \\n275: \\t\\tselect watches with already pending event data\\n285: func (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\\n286: \\ts.mu.Lock()\\n287: \\tvictims := s.victims\\n288: \\ts.victims = nil\\n289: \\ts.mu.Unlock()\\n290: \\n291: \\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\\n292: \\tfor _, wb := range victims {\\n293: \\t\\t// try to send responses again\\n294: \\t\\tfor w, eb := range wb {\\n295: \\t\\t\\t// watchers from the unsynced watcher group\\n343: //  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\\n344: //  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\\n345: //  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\\n346: func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\\n347: \\ts.mu.Lock()\\n348: \\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\\n349: \\n350: \\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\\n351: \\t\\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\\n352: \\t}\\n353: \\n354: \\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\\n355: \\tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\\n356: \\n357: \\t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced watchers, we need to\\n358: \\t// find min revision index, and \\n416: // rangeEventsWithReuse returns events in range [minRev, maxRev), while reusing already provided events.\\n417: func rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, \\t\\tsuffixIndex--\\n443: \\t}\\n444: \\tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\\n445: \\treturn evs\\n446: }\\n447: \\n448: // rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\\n449: func rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\\n450: \\tif minRev < 0 {\\n451: \\t\\tlg.Warn(\\\"Unexpected negative revision range start\\\", zap.Int64(\\\"minRev\\\", \\tfor {\\n162: \\t\\ts.mu.Lock()\\n163: \\t\\tif s.unsynced.delete(wa) {\\n164: \\t\\t\\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\\n165: \\t\\t\\twatcherGauge.Dec()\\n166: \\t\\t\\tbreak\\n167: \\t\\t} else if syncWatchersLoop syncs the watcher in the unsynced map every 100ms.\\n223: func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchersLoop() {\\n224: \\tdefer s.wg.Done()\\n225: \\n226: \\tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\\n227: \\tdefer delayTicker.Stop()\\n228: \\tvar evs []mvccpb.Event\\n229: \\n230: \\tfor {\\n231: \\t\\ts.mu.RLock()\\n232: \\t\\tst := time.Now()\\n233: \\t\\t}\\n248: \\n249: \\t\\tselect {\\n250: \\t\\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\\n251: \\t\\tcase <-s.stopc:\\n252: \\t\\t\\treturn\\n253: \\t\\t}\\n254: \\t}\\n255: }\\n256: \\n257: // syncVictimsLoop tries {\\n276: \\t\\tcase <-tickc:\\n277: \\t\\tcase <-s.victimc:\\n278: \\t\\tcase <-s.stopc:\\n279: \\t\\t\\treturn\\n280: \\t\\t}\\n281: \\t}\\n282: }\\n283: \\n284: // moveVictims tries to update watches with already pending event data\\n285: func (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\\n286: \\ts.mu.Lock()\\n287: \\tvictims := s.victims\\n288: \\ts.victims = nil\\n289: \\ts.mu.Unlock()\\n290: \\n291: \\tvar newVictim watcherBatch\\n292: \\tfor _, wb := range victims {\\n293: \\t\\t// try to send responses again\\n294: \\t\\tfor w, eb := range wb {\\n295: \\t\\t\\t// send those events to watchers\\n345: //  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\\n346: func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\\n347: \\ts.mu.Lock()\\n348: \\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\\n349: \\n350: \\tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\\n351: \\t\\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\\n352: \\t}\\n353: \\n354: \\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\\n355: \\tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\\n356: \\n357: \\t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced watchers, we need to\\n358: \\t// find min revision index, and \\n416: // rangeEventsWithReuse returns events in range [minRev, maxRev), while reusing already provided events.\\n417: func rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\\n418: \\tif len(evs) == 0 {\\n419: \\t\\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\\n420: \\t}\\n421: \\t// append from left\\n422: \\tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision \\t\\tsuffixIndex--\\n443: \\t}\\n444: \\tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\\n445: \\treturn evs\\n446: }\\n447: \\n448: // rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\\n449: func rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\\n450: \\tif minRev < 0 {\\n451: \\t\\tlg.Warn(\\\"Unexpected negative revision range start\\\", zap.Int64(\\\"minRev\\\", \tchanBufLen = 128\n38: \n39: \t// maxWatchersPerSync is the number of watchers to sync in a single batch\n40: \tmaxWatchersPerSync = 512\n41: \n42: \t// maxResyncPeriod is the period of executing int64, id WatchID, ch chan<- WatchResponse, fcs ...FilterFunc) (*watcher, cancelFunc)\n50: \tprogress(w *watcher)\n51: \tprogressAll(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher) bool\n52: \trev() int64\n53: }\n54: \n55: type watchableStore struct {\n56: \t*store\n57: \n58: \t// mu protects watcher groups and batches. It should never be locked\n59: \t// before locking store.mu to avoid deadlock.\n60: \tmu sync.RWMutex\n61: \n62: \t// victims are watcher batches that were blocked on the watch channel\n63: \tvictims synced watchers that are in sync with the progress of the store.\n70: \t// The key of the map is the key that the watcher watches on.\n71: \tsynced watcherGroup\n72: \n73: \tstopc chan struct{}\n74: \twg    sync.WaitGroup\n75: }\n76: \n77: var _ WatchableKV = (*watchableStore)(nil)\n78: \n79: // cancelFunc updates unsynced and synced maps when running\n80: // cancel operations.\n81: type cancelFunc func()\n82: \n83: func New(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, le lease.Lessor, cfg StoreConfig) WatchableKV {\n84: \ts := newWatchableStore(lg, b, le, cfg)\n85: \ts.wg.Add(2)\n86: \tgo s.syncWatchersLoop()\n87: \tgo s.syncVictimsLoop()\n88: \treturn s\n89: }\n90: \n91: func newWatchableStore(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, le lease.Lessor, cfg StoreConfig) *watchableStore {\n92: \tif lg == nil {\n93: \t\tlg = zap.NewNop()\n94: \t}\n95: \ts := &watchableStore{\n96: \t\tstore:    NewStore(lg, b, le, cfg),\n97: \t\tvictimc:  make(chan struct{}, 1),\n98: \t\tunsynced: NewWatchStream() WatchStream {\n118: \twatchStreamGauge.Inc()\n119: \treturn &watchStream{\n120: \t\twatchable: s,\n121: \t\tch:        make(chan WatchResponse, chanBufLen),\n122: \t\tcancels: WatchResponse, fcs ...FilterFunc) (*watcher, cancelFunc) {\n128: \twa := &watcher{\n129: \t\tkey:      key,\n130: \t\tend:      end,\n131: \t\tstartRev: startRev,\n132: \t\tminRev:   startRev,\n133: \t\tslowWatcherGauge.Inc()\n149: \t\ts.unsynced.add(wa)\n150: \t}\n151: \ts.revMu.RUnlock()\n152: \ts.mu.Unlock()\n153: \n154: \twatcherGauge.Inc()\n155: \n156: \treturn wa, func() { s.cancelWatcher(wa) }\n157: }\n158: \n159: // cancelWatcher removes references of the watcher from the watchableStore\n160: func (s *watchableStore) cancelWatcher(wa *watcher) {\n161: \tfor {\n162: \t\ts.mu.Lock()\n163: \t\tif s.unsynced.delete(wa) {\n164: \t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n165: \t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n166: \t\t\tbreak\n167: \t\t} else if s.synced.delete(wa) {\n168: \t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n169: \t\t\tbreak\n170: \t\t} else if wa.ch == nil {\n171: \t\t\t// already canceled (e.g., cancel/close race)\n172: \t\t\tbreak\n173: \t\t} else if wa.compacted {\n174: \t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n175: \t\t\tbreak\n176: \t\t}\n177: \n178: \t\tif !wa.victim {\n179: \t\t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n180: \t\t\tpanic(\"watcher not victim but not in watch groups\")\n181: \t\t}\n182: \t\tif victimBatch != nil {\n191: \t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n192: \t\t\twatcherGauge.Dec()\n193: \t\t\tdelete(victimBatch, wa)\n194: \t\t\tbreak\n195: \t\t}\n196: \n197: \t\t// victim being processed so not accessible; retry\n198: \t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n199: \t\ttime.Sleep(time.Millisecond)\n200: \t}\n201: \n202: \twa.ch = nil\n203: \ts.mu.Unlock()\n204: }\n205: \n206: func (s *watchableStore) Restore(b backend.Backend) error {\n207: \ts.mu.Lock()\n208: \tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n209: \terr := s.store.Restore(b)\n210: \tif err != nil {\n211: \t\treturn err\n212: \t}\n213: \n214: \tfor wa := range s.synced.watchers {\n215: \t\twa.restore = true\n216: \t\ts.unsynced.add(wa)\n217: \t}\n218: \ts.synced = newWatcherGroup()\n219: \treturn nil\n220: }\n221: \n222: // syncWatchersLoop syncs the watcher in the unsynced map every 100ms.\n223: func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchersLoop() {\n224: \tdefer s.wg.Done()\n225: \n226: \tdelayTicker := time.NewTicker(watchResyncPeriod)\n227: \tdefer delayTicker.Stop()\n228: \tvar evs []mvccpb.Event\n229: \n230: \tfor {\n231: \t\ts.mu.RLock()\n232: \t\tst := time.Now()\n233: \t\tlastUnsyncedWatchers \t\tsyncDuration := time.Since(st)\n241: \n242: \t\tdelayTicker.Reset(watchResyncPeriod)\n243: \t\t// more work pending?\n244: \t\tif unsyncedWatchers != 0 && lastUnsyncedWatchers > unsyncedWatchers {\n245: \t\t\t// be fair to other store operations by yielding time taken\n246: \t\t\tdelayTicker.Reset(syncDuration)\n247: \t\t}\n248: \n249: \t\tselect {\n250: \t\tcase <-delayTicker.C:\n251: \t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n252: \t\t\treturn\n253: \t\t}\n254: \t}\n255: }\n256: \n257: // syncVictimsLoop tries to write precomputed watcher responses to\n258: // watchers that had a blocked watcher channel\n259: func (s *watchableStore) syncVictimsLoop() {\n260: \tdefer s.wg.Done()\n261: \n262: \tfor {\n263: \t\tfor s.moveVictims() != 0 {\n264: \t\t\t// try to update all victim watchers\n265: \t\t}\n266: \t\ts.mu.RLock()\n267: \t\tisEmpty := len(s.victims) == 0\n268: \t\ts.mu.RUnlock()\n269: \n270: \t\tvar tickc <-chan time.Time\n271: \t\tif !isEmpty {\n272: \t\t\ttickc = time.After(10 * time.Millisecond)\n273: \t\t}\n274: \n275: \t\tselect {\n276: \t\tcase <-tickc:\n277: \t\tcase <-s.victimc:\n278: \t\tcase <-s.stopc:\n279: \t\t\treturn\n280: \t\t}\n281: \t}\n282: }\n283: \n284: // moveVictims tries to update watches with already pending event data\n285: func (s *watchableStore) moveVictims() (moved int) {\n286: \ts.mu.Lock()\n287: \tvictims := s.victims\n288: \ts.victims = nil\n289: \ts.mu.Unlock()\n290: \n291: \tvar newVictim watcherBatch\n292: \tfor _, wb := range victims {\n293: \t\t// try to send responses again\n294: \t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n295: \t\t\t// watcher has observed the store up to, but not including, w.minRev\n296: \t\t\trev := w.minRev - 1\n297: \t\t\tif !w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n298: \t\t\t\tif newVictim == nil {\n299: \t\t\t\t\tnewVictim = make(watcherBatch)\n300: \t\t\t\t}\n301: \t\t\t\tnewVictim[w] = eb\n302: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n303: \t\t\t}\n304: \t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n305: \t\t\tmoved++\n306: \t\t}\n307: \n308: \t\t// assign completed victim watchers to unsync/sync\n309: \t\ts.mu.Lock()\n310: \t\ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n311: \t\tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n312: \t\tfor w, eb := range wb {\n313: \t\t\tif newVictim != nil && newVictim[w] != nil {\n314: \t\t\t\t// couldn't send watch response; stays victim\n315: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n316: \t\t\t}\n317: \t\t\tw.victim = false\n318: \t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n319: \t\t\t\tw.minRev = eb.moreRev\n320: \t\t\t}\n321: \t\t\tif w.minRev <= curRev {\n322: \t\t\t\ts.unsynced.add(w)\n323: \t\t\t} else {\n324: \t\t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Dec()\n325: \t\t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n326: \t\t\t}\n327: \t\t}\n328: \t\ts.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n329: \t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n330: \t}\n331: \n332: \tif len(newVictim) > 0 {\n333: \t\ts.mu.Lock()\n334: \t\ts.victims = append(s.victims, newVictim)\n335: \t\ts.mu.Unlock()\n336: \t}\n337: \n338: \treturn moved\n339: }\n340: \n341: // syncWatchers syncs unsynced watchers by:\n342: //  1. choose a set of watchers from the unsynced watcher group\n343: //  2. iterate over the set to get the minimum revision and remove compacted watchers\n344: //  3. use minimum revision to get all key-value pairs and send those events to watchers\n345: //  4. remove synced watchers in set from unsynced group and move to synced group\n346: func (s *watchableStore) syncWatchers(evs []mvccpb.Event) (int, []mvccpb.Event) {\n347: \ts.mu.Lock()\n348: \tdefer s.mu.Unlock()\n349: \n350: \tif s.unsynced.size() == 0 {\n351: \t\treturn 0, []mvccpb.Event{}\n352: \t}\n353: \n354: \ts.store.revMu.RLock()\n355: \tdefer s.store.revMu.RUnlock()\n356: \n357: \t// in order to find key-value pairs from unsynced watchers, we need to\n358: \t// find min revision index, and these revisions can be used to\n359: \t// query the backend store of key-value pairs\n360: \tcurRev := s.store.currentRev\n361: \tcompactionRev := s.store.compactMainRev\n362: \n363: \twg, minRev := s.unsynced.choose(maxWatchersPerSync, curRev, compactionRev)\n364: \tevs = rangeEventsWithReuse(s.store.lg, s.store.b, evs, minRev, curRev+1)\n365: \n366: \tvictims := make(watcherBatch)\n367: \twb := newWatcherBatch(wg, evs)\n368: \tfor w := range wg.watchers {\n369: \t\tif w.minRev < compactionRev {\n370: \t\t\t// Skip the watcher that failed to send compacted watch response due to w.ch is full.\n371: \t\t\t// Next retry of syncWatchers would try to resend the compacted watch response to w.ch\n372: \t\t\tcontinue\n373: \t\t}\n374: \t\tw.minRev = max(curRev+1, w.minRev)\n375: \n376: \t\teb, ok := wb[w]\n377: \t\tif !ok {\n378: \t\t\t// bring un-notified watcher to synced\n379: \t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n380: \t\t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n381: \t\t\tcontinue\n382: \t\t}\n383: \n384: \t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n385: \t\t\tw.minRev = eb.moreRev\n386: \t\t}\n387: \n388: \t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: curRev}) {\n389: \t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n390: \t\t} else {\n391: \t\t\tw.victim = true\n392: \t\t}\n393: \n394: \t\tif w.victim {\n395: \t\t\tvictims[w] = eb\n396: \t\t} else {\n397: \t\t\tif eb.moreRev != 0 {\n398: \t\t\t\t// stay unsynced; more to read\n399: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n400: \t\t\t}\n401: \t\t\ts.synced.add(w)\n402: \t\t}\n403: \t\ts.unsynced.delete(w)\n404: \t}\n405: \ts.addVictim(victims)\n406: \n407: \tvsz := 0\n408: \tfor _, v := range s.victims {\n409: \t\tvsz += len(v)\n410: \t}\n411: \tslowWatcherGauge.Set(float64(s.unsynced.size() + vsz))\n412: \n413: \treturn s.unsynced.size(), evs\n414: }\n415: \n416: // rangeEventsWithReuse returns events in range [minRev, maxRev), while reusing already provided events.\n417: func rangeEventsWithReuse(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, evs []mvccpb.Event, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n418: \tif len(evs) == 0 {\n419: \t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n420: \t}\n421: \t// append from left\n422: \tif evs[0].Kv.ModRevision > minRev {\n423: \t\tevs = append(rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, evs[0].Kv.ModRevision), evs...)\n424: \t}\n425: \t// cut from left\n426: \tprefixIndex := 0\n427: \tfor prefixIndex < len(evs) && evs[prefixIndex].Kv.ModRevision < minRev {\n428: \t\tprefixIndex++\n429: \t}\n430: \tevs = evs[prefixIndex:]\n431: \n432: \tif len(evs) == 0 {\n433: \t\treturn rangeEvents(lg, b, minRev, maxRev)\n434: \t}\n435: \t// append from right\n436: \tif evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1 < maxRev {\n437: \t\tevs = append(evs, rangeEvents(lg, b, evs[len(evs)-1].Kv.ModRevision+1, maxRev)...)\n438: \t}\n439: \t// cut from right\n440: \tsuffixIndex := len(evs) - 1\n441: \tfor suffixIndex >= 0 && evs[suffixIndex].Kv.ModRevision >= maxRev {\n442: \t\tsuffixIndex--\n443: \t}\n444: \tevs = evs[:suffixIndex+1]\n445: \treturn evs\n446: }\n447: \n448: // rangeEvents returns events in range [minRev, maxRev).\n449: func rangeEvents(lg *zap.Logger, b backend.Backend, minRev, maxRev int64) []mvccpb.Event {\n450: \tif minRev < 0 {\n451: \t\tlg.Warn(\"Unexpected negative revision range start\", zap.Int64(\"minRev\", minRev))\n452: \t\tminRev = 0\n453: \t}\n454: \tminBytes, maxBytes := NewRevBytes(), NewRevBytes()\n455: \tminBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: minRev}, minBytes)\n456: \tmaxBytes = RevToBytes(Revision{Main: maxRev}, maxBytes)\n457: \n458: \t// UnsafeRange returns keys and values. And in boltdb, keys are revisions.\n459: \t// values are actual key-value pairs in backend.\n460: \ttx := b.ReadTx()\n461: \ttx.RLock()\n462: \trevs, vs := tx.UnsafeRange(schema.Key, minBytes, maxBytes, 0)\n463: \tevs := kvsToEvents(lg, revs, vs)\n464: \t// Must unlock after kvsToEvents, because vs (come from boltdb memory) is not deep copy.\n465: \t// We can only unlock after Unmarshal, which will do deep copy.\n466: \t// Otherwise we will trigger SIGSEGV during boltdb re-mmap.\n467: \ttx.RUnlock()\n468: \treturn evs\n469: }\n470: \n471: // kvsToEvents gets all events for the watchers from all key-value pairs\n472: func kvsToEvents(lg *zap.Logger, revs, vals [][]byte) (evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n473: \tfor i, v := range vals {\n474: \t\tvar kv mvccpb.KeyValue\n475: \t\tif err := kv.Unmarshal(v); err != nil {\n476: \t\t\tlg.Panic(\"failed to unmarshal mvccpb.KeyValue\", zap.Error(err))\n477: \t\t}\n478: \n479: \t\tty := mvccpb.Event_PUT\n480: \t\tif isTombstone(revs[i]) {\n481: \t\t\tty = mvccpb.Event_DELETE\n482: \t\t\t// patch in mod revision so watchers won't skip\n483: \t\t\tkv.ModRevision = BytesToRev(revs[i]).Main\n484: \t\t}\n485: \t\tevs = append(evs, mvccpb.Event{Kv: &kv, Type: ty})\n486: \t}\n487: \treturn evs\n488: }\n489: \n490: // notify notifies the fact that given event at the given rev just happened to\n491: // watchers that watch on the key of the event.\n492: func (s *watchableStore) notify(rev int64, evs []mvccpb.Event) {\n493: \tvictim := make(watcherBatch)\n494: \tfor w, eb := range newWatcherBatch(&s.synced, evs) {\n495: \t\tif eb.revs != 1 {\n496: \t\t\ts.store.lg.Panic(\n497: \t\t\t\t\"unexpected multiple revisions in watch notification\",\n498: \t\t\t\tzap.Int(\"number-of-revisions\", eb.revs),\n499: \t\t\t)\n500: \t\t}\n501: \t\tif w.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: w.id, Events: eb.evs, Revision: rev}) {\n502: \t\t\tpendingEventsGauge.Add(float64(len(eb.evs)))\n503: \t\t} else {\n504: \t\t\t// move slow watcher to victims\n505: \t\t\tw.victim = true\n506: \t\t\tvictim[w] = eb\n507: \t\t\ts.synced.delete(w)\n508: \t\t\tslowWatcherGauge.Inc()\n509: \t\t}\n510: \t\t// always update minRev\n511: \t\t// in case 'send' returns true and watcher stays synced, this is needed for Restore when all watchers become unsynced\n512: \t\t// in case 'send' returns false, this is needed for syncWatchers\n513: \t\tw.minRev = rev + 1\n514: \t}\n515: \ts.addVictim(victim)\n516: }\n517: \n518: func (s *watchableStore) addVictim(victim watcherBatch) {\n519: \tif len(victim) == 0 {\n520: \t\treturn\n521: \t}\n522: \ts.victims = append(s.victims, victim)\n523: \tselect {\n524: \tcase s.victimc <- struct{}{}:\n525: \tdefault:\n526: \t}\n527: }\n528: \n529: func (s *watchableStore) rev() int64 { return s.store.Rev() }\n530: \n531: func (s *watchableStore) progress(w *watcher) {\n532: \ts.progressIfSync(map[WatchID]*watcher{w.id: w}, w.id)\n533: }\n534: \n535: func (s *watchableStore) progressAll(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher) bool {\n536: \treturn s.progressIfSync(watchers, clientv3.InvalidWatchID)\n537: }\n538: \n539: func (s *watchableStore) progressIfSync(watchers map[WatchID]*watcher, responseWatchID WatchID) bool {\n540: \ts.mu.RLock()\n541: \tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()\n542: \n543: \trev := s.rev()\n544: \t// Any watcher unsynced?\n545: \tfor _, w := range watchers {\n546: \t\tif _, ok := s.synced.watchers[w]; !ok {\n547: \t\t\treturn false\n548: \t\t}\n549: \t\tif rev < w.startRev {\n550: \t\t\treturn false\n551: \t\t}\n552: \t}\n553: \n554: \t// If all watchers are synchronised, send out progress\n555: \t// notification on first watcher. Note that all watchers\n556: \t// should have the same underlying stream, and the progress\n557: \t// notification will be broadcasted client-side if required\n558: \t// (see dispatchEvent in client/v3/watch.go)\n559: \tfor _, w := range watchers {\n560: \t\tw.send(WatchResponse{WatchID: responseWatchID, Revision: rev})\n561: \t\treturn true\n562: \t}\n563: \treturn true\n564: }\n565: \n566: type watcher struct {\n567: \t// the watcher key\n568: \tkey []byte\n569: \t// end indicates the end of the range to watch.\n570: \t// If end is set, the watcher is on a range.\n571: \tend []byte\n572: \n573: \t// victim is set when ch is blocked and undergoing victim processing\n574: \tvictim bool\n575: \n576: \t// compacted is set when the watcher is removed because of compaction\n577: \tcompacted bool\n578: \n579: \t// restore is true when the watcher is being restored from leader snapshot\n580: \t// which means that this watcher has just been moved from \"synced\" to \"unsynced\"\n581: \t// watcher group, possibly with a future revision when it was first added\n582: \t// to the synced watcher\n583: \t// \"unsynced\" watcher revision must always be <= current context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n62: \treturn pc\n63: }\n64: \n65: /*\n66: Compaction period 1-hour:\n67:   1. compute compaction period, which is 1-hour\n68:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\n69:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 1-hour\n70:   4. do compact with revs[0]\n71: \t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n72: \t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 1-hour (6-minute)\n73: \n74: Compaction period 24-hour:\n75:   1. compute compaction period, which is 24-hour\n76:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 24-hour (144-minute)\n77:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 24-hour\n78:   4. do compact with revs[0]\n79: \t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n80: \t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 24-hour (144-minute)\n81: \n82: Compaction period 59-min:\n83:   1. compute compaction period, which is 59-min\n84:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 59-min (5.9-min)\n85:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 59-min\n86:   4. do compact with revs[0]\n87: \t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n88: \t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 59-min (5.9-min)\n89: \n90: Compaction period 5-sec:\n91:   1. compute compaction period, which is 5-sec\n92:   2. record revisions for every 1/10 of 5-sec (0.5-sec)\n93:   3. keep recording revisions with no compaction for first 5-sec\n94:   4. do compact with revs[0]\n95: \t- success? continue on for-loop and move sliding window; revs = revs[1:]\n96: \t- failure? update revs, and retry after 1/10 of 5-sec (0.5-sec)\n97: */\n98: \n99: // Run runs periodic compactor.\n100: func (pc *Periodic) Run() {\n101: \tcompactInterval := pc.getCompactInterval()\n102: \tretryInterval := pc.getRetryInterval()\n103: \tretentions := pc.getRetentions()\n104: \n105: \tgo func() {\n106: \t\tlastRevision := int64(0)\n107: \t\tlastSuccess := pc.clock.Now()\n108: \t\tbaseInterval := pc.period\n109: \t\tfor {\n110: \t\t\tpc.revs = append(pc.revs, pc.rg.Rev())\n111: \t\t\tif len(pc.revs) > retentions {\n112: \t\t\t\tpc.revs = pc.revs[1:] // pc.revs[0] is always the rev at pc.period ago\n113: \t\t\t}\n114: \n115: \t\t\tselect {\n116: \t\t\tcase <-pc.ctx.Done():\n117: \t\t\t\treturn\n118: \t\t\tcase <-pc.clock.After(retryInterval):\n119: \t\t\t\tpc.mu.RLock()\n120: \t\t\t\tp := pc.paused\n121: \t\t\t\tpc.mu.RUnlock()\n122: \t\t\t\tif p {\n123: \t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n124: \t\t\t\t}\n125: \t\t\t}\n126: \t\t\trev := pc.revs[0]\n127: \t\t\tif pc.clock.Now().Sub(lastSuccess) < baseInterval || rev == lastRevision {\n128: \t\t\t\tcontinue\n129: \t\t\t}\n130: \n131: \t\t\t// wait up to initial given period\n132: \t\t\tif baseInterval == pc.period {\n133: \t\t\t\tbaseInterval = compactInterval\n134: \t\t\t}\n135: \n136: \t\t\tpc.lg.Info(\n137: \t\t\t\t\"starting auto periodic compaction\",\n138: \t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n139: \t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"compact-period\", pc.period),\n140: \t\t\t)\n141: \t\t\tstartTime := pc.clock.Now()\n142: \t\t\t_, err := pc.c.Compact(pc.ctx, &pb.CompactionRequest{Revision: rev})\n143: \t\t\tif err == nil || errors.Is(err, mvcc.ErrCompacted) {\n144: \t\t\t\tpc.lg.Info(\n145: \t\t\t\t\t\"completed auto periodic compaction\",\n146: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n147: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"compact-period\", pc.period),\n148: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"took\", pc.clock.Now().Sub(startTime)),\n149: \t\t\t\t)\n150: \t\t\t\tlastRevision = rev\n151: \t\t\t\tlastSuccess = pc.clock.Now()\n152: \t\t\t} else {\n153: \t\t\t\tpc.lg.Warn(\n154: \t\t\t\t\t\"failed auto periodic compaction\",\n155: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Int64(\"revision\", rev),\n156: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"compact-period\", pc.period),\n157: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Duration(\"retry-interval\", retryInterval),\n158: \t\t\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n159: \t\t\t\t)\n160: \t\t\t}\n161: \t\t}\n162: \t}()\n163: }\n164: \n165: // if given compaction period x is <1-hour, compact every x duration.\n166: // (e.g. --auto-compaction-mode 'periodic' --auto-compaction-retention='10m', then compact every 10-minute)\n167: // if given compaction period x is >1-hour, compact every hour.\n168: // (e.g. --auto-compaction-mode 'periodic' --auto-compaction-retention='2h', then compact every 1-hour)\n169: func (pc *Periodic) getCompactInterval() time.Duration {\n170: \titv := pc.period\n171: \tif itv > time.Hour {\n172: \t\titv = time.Hour\n173: \t}\n174: \treturn itv\n175: }\n176: \n177: func (pc *Periodic) getRetentions() int {\n178: \treturn int(pc.period/pc.getRetryInterval()) + 1\n179: }\n180: \n181: const retryDivisor = 10\n182: \n183: func (pc *Periodic) getRetryInterval() time.Duration {\n184: \titv := pc.period\n185: \tif itv > time.Hour {\n186: \t\titv = time.Hour\n187: \t}\n188: \treturn itv / retryDivisor\n189: }\n190: \n191: // Stop stops periodic compactor.\n192: func (pc *Periodic) Stop() {\n193: \tpc.cancel()\n194: }\n195: \n196: // Pause pauses periodic compactor.\n197: func (pc *Periodic) Pause() {\n198: \tpc.mu.Lock()\n199: \tpc.paused = true\n200: \tpc.mu.Unlock()\n201: }\n202: \n203: // Resume resumes periodic compactor.\n204: func (pc *Periodic) Resume() {\n205: \tpc.mu.Lock()\n206: \tpc.paused = false\n207: \tpc.mu.Unlock()\n208: }\n209:
